style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >是故天生神物，圣人则之；天地变化，圣人故之；天垂象见吉凶，圣人象之；河出《图》，洛出《书》，圣人则之。</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#8221;</span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >。河图之象</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65380;</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >之数</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65380;</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >之理</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65380;</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >至简至易，又深邃无穷。暂且论之。</font></span></i><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span></i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >相关派系</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：能量、命运、时空、力场、灵性</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >特殊</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：在获得河图洛书时，可以选择获得真气而非魔力，若如此做，其记载的法术视为修真系统法术，以真气而非魔力使用，且法术体系同时视为仙术。在判断其他与施法者职能相关的特性及其前提时，该真气可以被视作魔力。这个选择必须在购买时做出，并且无法更改。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >本体</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-align:left;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >河图洛书没有本体</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#8212;&#8212;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >或者说，主神空间中的复本河图洛书没有本体。取而代之的，人物领悟了记载于天书中浩瀚无穷的天地之道。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >当魔导书达到</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >A</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级时，人物一次性获得</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >36</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点经验值，这个经验只能用来自创技能。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span >人物的手背上浮现四象刻印。每类刻印均会为人物提供相应的属性加值和等量的检定加值，并在施法时显现不同颜色的幽光。人物只能使用一个刻印，但可以使用一个移动动作来更改刻印的类型。刻印所带来的加值均为额外的机运加值。</font></span><span >四象刻印变得更为清晰，现在施法时神兽的虚影会在人物周围飞舞。在此等级，刻印的属性加值和检定加值提升，并额外提供等量的附加成功加值。此外，人物可以使用一个迅捷动作来更改刻印的类型。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >+4</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >，力量</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >+2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >，沉着</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >+2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >鬼械神</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >河图洛书没有鬼械神，而以『河图洛书混元大阵』取而代之。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >河图洛书混元大阵，由十万八千年内所有的符文及先天灵宝河图洛书组合而成的绝对防御，本质为混沌气息，通过河图洛书阴阳相合，逆转了两仪之势，反逆时空，重回混沌，扭转了时间线，空间线，能量线，物质线的四大元素防御体系，因果率的最高级招式，任何攻击到达之时，都将逆转阴阳，逆转因果，最终彻底无效的终极防御体系。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >使用</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >个整轮动作开启，在开启阵势之时，施法者受到咒力圈的保护，如同召唤</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65378;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >鬼械神</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65379;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >。此外，施法者可以同时施展若干个类别为物质、能量、时空或力场，施法时间不超过整轮，且目标包含自身的法术，这些法术有如下不同：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;无需施法动作，忽视所有成分</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;目标改为『河图洛书混元大阵』</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;持续时间改为永久或直至阵势解消</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;每个法术需要额外支付</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >9</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点魔力</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >在成型之后每维持一轮，施法者都会消耗</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >9</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点魔力和</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >3</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点意志，这魔力不能由魔导书支付。在展开阵势的状态下将意志消耗完时，人物会直接化为鸿蒙气息而消散。以一个标准动作，施法者可以解散『河图洛书混元大阵』，将其还原为符文。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >特殊的，人物可以花费</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >10</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >魔力和</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >10</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >意志和</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >10</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >分钟时间，提前准备好这个阵势并维持不散发，最多持续九个时辰（</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >18</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >小时）。在已准备的情况下，可以一个反射动作使用，以此法展开的河图洛书混元大阵只能到你下个回合开始，之后便需要重新准备。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >展开阵势时，施法者可以正常施展其拥有的法术，但是不能移动。每一次攻击和施法，都会额外消耗</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点意志。在维持河图洛书混元大阵时，施法者只具有标准动作。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >『河图洛书混元大阵』被视为体积为</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >50</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >的物体，具有</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >49</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点基础防御，</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >49</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点力场防御以及</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >49</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点幸运防御，具有相当于施法者感知值的快速医疗和决心值的全伤害吸收，其生命值为</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >100</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >，再加上施法者的风度值。以一个标准动作，施法者可以调节『河图洛书混元大阵』体积，但必须笼罩施法者本身，且至多不能超过</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >100</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >，这不会带来相关属性的变化。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >若施法者以标准动作进行全防御，『河图洛书混元大阵』同样视为进行了全防御，并且因施法者属性而获得的快速医疗和全伤害吸收变为原先的两倍。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >当角色被阵势所笼罩时，其所进行的对抗</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65380;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >抵御与防御直接使用『河图洛书混元大阵』的数值，受到的伤害也改为扣除阵势的生命值。如果需要承受范围攻击，那么视为只有『河图洛书混元大阵』受到了这次攻击的影响。若『河图洛书混元大阵』需要进行检定，改为使用施法者的意志，但后果由阵势本身承受。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65378;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >八卦阵</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65379;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >，放出虹色的能量轰击前方的目标。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-align:left;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >以施法检定发起一次远程能量攻击，并额外获得威力值的附加成功数，这是纯粹能量加值。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >这道法术造成严重伤害，这属于能量伤害，可以被有抵抗能量伤害特性的护甲转化为冲击，也可以被能量抗力吸收。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-align:left;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >D</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级以上的每个法术等级，施法者可以从以下八种能量类型选择一种获得之：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="margin-left:21.0000pt;text-align:left;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >灼热，冻寒，电击，腐蚀，音波，光能，正能量，负能量</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-align:left;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >在判断该法术产生的伤害和加值类型时，取已附加能量类型中较有利的一种。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >增幅</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：支付</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >4</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点魔力，使得该法术获得『能量武器』特性。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-align:left;" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >研发</font></span></b><span >此法术能够让施法者感知能量及其变化。在该法术生效期间，人物可以在上述的行动中以施法检定取代调查检定，并在此类检定上额外获得如同威力值的洞察加值。这同时视为法术等级的魔幻本质侦测效果。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >D1C2B3A4S5</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >）相同强度的灵光，而生物的灵光等级则取决于其具有的能量，具有多类能量的生物会散发出多种灵光，但在判断灵光等级时取其最高者，人物自动得知他所见灵光的等级。对于人物而言，等于魔导书等级的灵光称作中等灵光，低于</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >/</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >高于魔导书等级</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >强烈灵光，低于</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >/</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >DC</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-align:left;" ><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >增幅</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：支付</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >4</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >10</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >成功数，无须专注。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >D+500</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >现在，人物可以分辨出不同类型的能量所散发不同色灵光，具体颜色自行设定。人物可以籍此辨识出能量的类型，即使并不了解这类能量，人物依然可以感受到该能量的特性。例如，河图洛书的等级为</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >B</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >时，对于一名</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >B</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级武斗家，施法者可以察觉到他体内充斥着一种介于内力与斗气之间的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65380;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >既不稳定也不狂暴的能量，并可以观察到中等橙色灵光（若设定气为橙色的话），而对于一把已储存有魔力的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >D</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >该法术有两种用法，在获得该法术时需要选择其中一种，并可以如同同级法术一般购买另一种。若人物同时习得了两种用法，他可以在施展这道法术时同时使用两种用法。若如此做，第一种用法提供的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65378;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >卦</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65379;</font></span><span >&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&nbsp;</span><span Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65379;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >施法者能够以下列两种方式使用卦：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;当人物进行某次行动时，可以支付</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >卦，重掷掷骰结果中至多不超过威力值个骰子。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-align:left;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;当人物所能感知的其他角色进行某次行动时，可以支付</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >卦，重掷掷骰结果中至多不超过威力值个骰子。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal  style="text-align:left;" ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >对于一次行动，人物只能消耗一次</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65378;</font></span><span Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65379;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >若</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65378;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >卦</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65379;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >未被用尽，该法术可以持续一个场景。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.5000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=MsoNormal style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >C</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级以上的每个施法者等级，可以支付</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点魔力，额外获得</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >2</span><span >&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span ><font face="宋体" >铜钱</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65380;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点魔力，举行一次至少持续</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >10</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >分钟的仪式并进行施法检定，每成功数可以将该法术的效果保留</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >10</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >分钟，所要预见的事件必须发生在法术的持续时间内。成功的施展该法术后，人物会窥见即将发生的某种可能性，并在人物真正处于彼时的所有检定或防御提供等同于施法成功数的洞察加值。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >使用该法术需要提供尽量明确的描述，并应遵循</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65378;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >无事不占，不动不占，不为同一事反复占问</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65379;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >的原则。若提供的描述不够精确，所预见到的事件将会被在范围内随机决定（例如预测</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65378;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >明日运势</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65379;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >会随机预见该日中某段时间，而</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65378;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >今日午时准点</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65379;</font></span><span Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65378;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >明日第一次挥刀时</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65379;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >则可以精准测定范围）。天机不可枉测，在法术效果结束前，人物无法再次进行占卜。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >可选：频繁的窥伺天机会导致不可知的灾祸发生，人物可以在确知这一点的情况下进行更多次占卜，但可能会使剧情向难以预知的情况发展，并且人物会因此被位面所排斥（一般表现为该世界中在检定上受到</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >-2DP/</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >占卜次数的机运减值，或是一场造成不超过施法成功数严重伤害的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65378;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >美丽意外</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65379;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >ST</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >也可以自行设定更加具体的效果。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >占卜完成后，人物会察觉到所使用的材料或周围环境（若免除了施法材料）上玄奥莫测的图案或现象（龟甲灼卜的纹路，五星连珠），成功通过一次智力</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >+</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >学识检定可以解读出更多的信息，具体的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >DC</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >ST</span><span Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65378;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >用九，见群龙无首，吉</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65379;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >，竹签的解）。但无论如何，人物至少会对该事件的运势有大概的了解，一般得到的答案如下：吉</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65380;</font></span><span ><font face="宋体" >吝</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65380;</font></span><span Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65380;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >悔</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65380;</font></span><span ><font face="宋体" >较人类具有更长寿命的长生种或拥有抵抗衰老能力的角色可以额外抵消</font></span><span >法术效果结束时，还原该法术所造成的所有效果，如同未施放这个法术一般。所有未使用完的临时生命和造成的伤害全部移除，但这不会使已死亡或失去意识的角色复活或者回复意识。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >《连山》者，象山之出云，连连不绝。施法者从高次投影意志，破坏并重构三维世界的空间法则，进行施法检定，该法术有以下两种使用方法：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >增幅：支付</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点魔力，人物可以将这个法术与冲锋或移动结合施展。以此法冲锋时，人物所需承受的防御减值减去施法成功数。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >若以此效果进行原来难以奏效的攻击时（包括无法触及目标的近战攻击以及承受距离减值的远程攻击），受攻击者视为处于如同法术等级的措手不及下。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >增幅</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：在以整轮动作施法时，施法者可将施法时间和持续时间提升</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级或多级，具体如下。施法者必须完成逐级完成这一增幅（例如，他在</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >10</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >轮施法中取得了</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >100</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >成功数，他可以将这</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >100</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >成功数作为</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >10</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >分钟中第</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >分钟的成功数，并继续进行周期为</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >分钟的施法检定）。施法判定以及受术者的意志判定因此（若受术者自愿或处于无助状态，则不进行意志判定）成为延长判定，合计最终取得的结果作为成功数。一旦开始，施法者就必须完成当级增幅，并且无法中断。若因任何意外因素中断施法，施法者立即</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65380;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >且不可避免的受到等同于当前周期施法成功数的冲击伤害。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span >&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;10</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >分钟</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#9;&nbsp;&nbsp;1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >封绝天地，截断神人之途，摧毁两界通道，只留昆仑一路。该法术有两种用法，在获得该法术时需要选择其中一种，并可以如同同级法术一般购买另一种。若人物同时习得了两种用法，他可以在施展这道法术时仅布置一个阵眼，但同时产生两种用法的效果。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >无论使用哪一种，都需要将阵眼（法术核心）布置在不超过</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >5</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >智力内的一个地点，一旦布置就不可再次变动，因此该法术具有【阵法】关键字。而其他生物需要通过一个</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >DC</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >+1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span >若阵眼被击破，则法术立即解消。该法术不会与自身的另一种用法互相干扰。若多个绝地天通在同一范围内作用，则施法者等级较高的一方生效；若双方等级相同，则较后施展的绝地天通生效。</font></span><span >&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >法术持续期间，区域内形成死魔区，任何在该范围内产生或影响</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >/</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >进入该范围的超自然效果都将被压制，这包括了下列效果：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;持续性效果：该法术等级以下的持续性效果（具有一个持续时间的效果）被自动压制。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;物品：除神兵外，所有低于该法术等级的</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65380;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >魔幻</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >/</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >特异本质的道具所提供的被动及主动效果全部失效，但它们依旧保有自身的特性（例如，一把失效的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65378;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >光轮</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65379;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >依旧视为大师级工匠弯刀）。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;能力：低于该法术三个等级以下的能力（包括被动能力）一应无法使用，但不会这些能力改变所带来的永久加值。低于该法术等级，但不低于该法术三个等级以下的主动能力在施展时（若对方不需要施展判定，则投意志）承受</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >成功数</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >/</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >威力的减值，而同等级的主动能力仅承受一半减值，高于该法术等级的能力不受影响。如果在施展时没有取得任何成功数，则该能力自动失败，且消耗的能量与材料不予返还。使用者可以支付额外的能量以抵消这一减值，每</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >能量抵消</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点减值。进入或影响区域内的效果同样受此影响，且无法抵消该减值。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;能量：进行能量池关键属性检定，所取得的成功数即为能在法术生效后至多保留的能量，剩余的能量将被压制，</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >D</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >C1B2A3S4</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >）在该检定上获得额外</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >5</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;召唤生物：如同持续性效果一般被压制。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >当法术效果解除后，所有被压制的持续性效果</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS ><font face="宋体" >能力和召唤生物受到法力虚空的解离作用，如同相应等级的法术</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:'MS Gothic';font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="MS Gothic" >&#65378;</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >解除魔法</font></span><span >&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&#8212;&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1/2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;持续性效果：所有持续性效果在引力场中每持续重力倍数轮视作</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >倍额外重力将延长</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >4</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点敏捷减值（不会降低到</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >以下），并降低</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >40</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点速度。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;飞行生物：进入区域内以及在区域内的每一轮，飞行生物需要通过</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >DC</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >为施法成功数的力量</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >+</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >运动检定，若失败则立即因其承受的每</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >倍额外重力下坠每失败数</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >5</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >米，若因此效果坠落到地面则视为倒地并承受坠落伤害。试图向上飞行的生物需要再进行一次对抗，其判定与后果如同前述，若在该对抗中胜出则可以正常向上飞行。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >投射物：所有在引力场中飞行的投射物（具有运动轨迹的物体，包括远程能量与实体攻击）的速度倍数减为当前时间流速，这会导致这些投射物因承受的每</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >倍额外重力而消耗</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >倍额外时间以达到目的地。不具有追踪能力的投射物可能因目标的移动而失手。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >人物也可以逆转引力场的方向，使其阻碍区域内的引力的产生，这使得重力减弱到原先的</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1/2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >，并致使范围内的时间流速变为</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >倍。这包含了下列效果：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;持续性效果：所有持续性效果所持续的每</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >轮视为持续了时间流速倍数轮，因此其真实持续时间变为原先的重力倍。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;物品：在判断负重（携带物品规则）和举重时，其真实重量等于原先的重量乘上重力倍数，并移除所有盔甲减值。此外，区域内不再产生坠物和坠落伤害。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;生物：因每</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >倍时间流速所带来而获得</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >4</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点敏捷加值，并提升</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >40</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点速度，这是速度加值。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;陆行生物：进入区域内以及在区域内的每一轮，陆行生物获得其基础速度乘上重力倍数的飞行速度，机动性为笨拙，并且因所承受的每</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >倍时间流速而自动上升施法成功数米，这是强制移动效果，某些架势或招式可能因此失效。若这些生物拥有飞行能力，可以选择更好的一项（但他们依旧只能飞行），而原先不具备飞行能力的生物被视为处于</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >A</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级措手不及状态下。这些生物可以做一个力量</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >+</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >运动检定对抗施法成功数以防止浮空，但失败会导致其因所承受的每</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >倍时间流速而上升每失败数</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >米，并在当轮内同样视作措手不及（即使它拥有飞行能力）。若需要向地面移动，这些生物再进行一次对抗，其判定与后果如同前述，若在该对抗中胜出则可以正常向下移动。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#183;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >投射物：所有在引力场中飞行的投射物的速度倍数增为当前时间流速，因此每</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >倍额外的时间流速使其获得高速</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >5</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >，这些好处只在引力场内生效。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >施法者可以进一步改变重力的倍数或比率，上限为每</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >8</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点威力值</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >个单位。该法术同时具有</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >[</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >时空</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >]</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >与</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >[</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >环境</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >]</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >描述，但除非同时免疫两者的干涉，否则该法术效果只有部分失效。空间原理的储物类道具在重力场中无法打开，但其内部的物品不会溢出或永久消失。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >增幅</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：施法者等级达到</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >S</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >级时，支付</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >3</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >意志和</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >9</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >魔力，可以使用反射动作使用或解消绝地天通，人物也可以一个反射动作逆转引力场的方向。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span
